(:define (domain alfred)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object - 
    microwaveReceptacle - receptacle
    sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
    fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (contained ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (handempty)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (used ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (not (opened ?r))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (opened ?r)
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (contained ?o ?r) (opened ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (not (contained ?o ?r)) (not (handempty)) (holding ?o))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (handempty) (contained ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?sharp_o) (contained ?co ?r))
    :effect (sliced ?co)
  )

  (:types
    receptacle object - 
    microwaveReceptacle - receptacle

    fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (contained ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (handempty)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (used ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (not (opened ?r))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (opened ?r)
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (contained ?o ?r) (opened ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (not (contained ?o ?r)) (not (handempty)) (holding ?o))
  )

    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))

  )

    :effect (used ?o)
  )

(define (domain alfred)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    object
    receptacle - object
    microwaveReceptacle - receptacle

    fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (contained ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (handempty)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (used ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (not (opened ?r))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (opened ?r)
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )

    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)

    :effect (and (not (contained ?o ?r)) (not (handempty)) (holding ?o))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (handempty) (contained ?o ?r))
  )

    :effect (used ?o)
  )

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain alfred)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    object
    receptacle - object
    microwaveReceptacle - receptacle
    sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
    fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (contained ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (handempty)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (used ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (not (opened ?r))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (opened ?r)
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (contained ?o ?r) (opened ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (not (contained ?o ?r)) (not (handempty)) (holding ?o))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (handempty) (contained ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?sharp_o) (contained ?co ?r))
    :effect (sliced ?co)
  )
)

This is previous problem file: 
(define (problem alfred-problem)
  (:domain alfred)
  (:objects
    bathtubbasin1 countertop1 drawer1 drawer2 drawer3 drawer4 drawer5 drawer6 garbagecan1 handtowelholder1 handtowelholder2 toilet1 toiletpaperhanger1 towelholder1 towelholder2 - receptacle
    sinkbasin1 sinkbasin2 - sinkbasinReceptacle
    toiletpaper1 - object
  )
  (:init
    (at drawer1)
    (handempty)
    (contained toiletpaper1 drawer2)
    (opened drawer1)
    (not (opened drawer2))
    (opened countertop1)
    (opened toiletpaperhanger1)
  )
  (:goal (at drawer2))
)

(define (domain alfred)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    object
    receptacle
    microwaveReceptacle - receptacle
    sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
    fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (contained ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (handempty)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (used ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (not (opened ?r))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (opened ?r)
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (contained ?o ?r) (opened ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (not (contained ?o ?r)) (not (handempty)) (holding ?o))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (handempty) (contained ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?sharp_o) (contained ?co ?r))
    :effect (sliced ?co)
  )
)

    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (not (opened ?r))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )

    :precondition (opened ?r)

  )

    :effect (and (not (contained ?o ?r)) (not (handempty)) (holding ?o))
  )

  )

(define (domain alfred)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    object
    receptacle
    microwaveReceptacle - receptacle
    sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
    fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (contained ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (handempty)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (used ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (not (opened ?r))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (opened ?r)
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (contained ?o ?r) (opened ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (not (contained ?o ?r)) (not (handempty)) (holding ?o))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (handempty) (contained ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain alfred)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    object
    receptacle
    microwaveReceptacle - receptacle
    sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
    fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (contained ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (handempty)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (used ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (not (opened ?r))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (opened ?r)
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (contained ?o ?r) (opened ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (not (contained ?o ?r)) (not (handempty)) (holding ?o))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (handempty) (contained ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?sharp_o) (contained ?co ?r))
    :effect (and (sliced ?co) (not (holding ?sharp_o)) (contained ?sharp_o ?r))
  )
)

(define (domain alfred)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    object
    receptacle
    microwaveReceptacle - receptacle
    sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
    fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (contained ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (handempty)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (used ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (not (opened ?r))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (opened ?r)
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (contained ?o ?r) (opened ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (not (contained ?o ?r)) (not (handempty)) (holding ?o))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (handempty) (contained ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain alfred)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    object
    receptacle
    microwaveReceptacle - receptacle
    sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
    fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (contained ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (handempty)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (used ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (not (opened ?r))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (opened ?r)
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (contained ?o ?r) (opened ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (not (contained ?o ?r)) (not (handempty)) (holding ?o))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (handempty) (contained ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?sharp_o) (contained ?co ?r))
    :effect (and (sliced ?co) (not (holding ?sharp_o)) (contained ?sharp_o ?r))
  )
)

  )
  (:init
    (at drawer1)
    (handempty)
    (opened drawer2)

    (opened drawer1)

  (:types
    object

    (sliced ?o - object)

  )

  )

    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )

    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (contained ?o ?r) (opened ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (not (contained ?o ?r)) (not (handempty)) (holding ?o))
  )

    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (handempty) (contained ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (used ?o)
  )

    :effect (heated ?o)
  )

  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    object
    receptacle

    sharpObject - object
  )

    (at ?r - receptacle)

    (contained ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (handempty)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)

    (sliced ?o - object)
    (used ?o - object)
  )

    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )

    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (not (opened ?r))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )

    :precondition (opened ?r)
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain alfred)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    object
    receptacle
    microwaveReceptacle - receptacle
    sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
    fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (contained ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (handempty)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (used ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (not (opened ?r))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (opened ?r)
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (contained ?o ?r) (opened ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (not (contained ?o ?r)) (not (handempty)) (holding ?o))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (handempty) (contained ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?sharp_o) (contained ?co ?r))
    :effect (and (sliced ?co) (not (holding ?sharp_o)) (contained ?sharp_o ?r))
  )
)

(define (domain alfred)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    object
    receptacle
    microwaveReceptacle - receptacle
    sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
    fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (contained ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (handempty)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (used ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (not (opened ?r))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (opened ?r)
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (contained ?o ?r) (opened ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (not (contained ?o ?r)) (not (handempty)) (holding ?o))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (handempty) (contained ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?sharp_o) (contained ?co ?r))
    :effect (and (sliced ?co) (not (holding ?sharp_o)) (contained ?sharp_o ?r))
  )
)

    :precondition (opened ?r)
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (contained ?o ?r) (opened ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (not (contained ?o ?r)) (not (handempty)) (holding ?o))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (handempty) (contained ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?sharp_o) (contained ?co ?r))
    :effect (and (sliced ?co) (not (holding ?sharp_o)) (contained ?sharp_o ?r))
  )
)

(define (domain alfred)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    object
    receptacle
    microwaveReceptacle - receptacle
    sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
    fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (contained ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (handempty)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (used ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (not (opened ?r))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (opened ?r)
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (contained ?o ?r) (opened ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (not (contained ?o ?r)) (not (handempty)) (holding ?o))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (handempty) (contained ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?sharp_o) (contained ?co ?r))
    :effect (and (sliced ?co) (not (holding ?sharp_o)) (contained ?sharp_o ?r))
  )
)

            1. If you want to heat, clean, and cool an object, after you go to that aim receptacle, do not put the object in the receptacle but do the action directly. For example, go to fridge, then cool the object with receptacle.

            3. If you want to examine or look at an object with a lamp, you should first go to the receptacle where the object is located and then pick it up and take the USE action of the lamp. You don't need to take the lamp but directly use it.
            4. If there are multiple actions needed to complete the task, you can break them down into smaller subgoals. For example, if you need to slice and then heat an object, first focus on slicing it, and then move on to heating it.

        In summary, the first stage is all about finding the object—this might involve going to an unvisited receptacle and opening it if necessary.

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain alfred)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    object
    receptacle
    microwaveReceptacle - receptacle
    sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
    fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (contained ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (handempty)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (used ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (not (opened ?r))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (opened ?r)
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (contained ?o ?r) (opened ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (not (contained ?o ?r)) (not (handempty)) (holding ?o))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (handempty) (contained ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?sharp_o) (contained ?co ?r))
    :effect (and (sliced ?co) (not (holding ?sharp_o)) (contained ?sharp_o ?r))
  )
)
